# feat2 vs beta — 24h Prometheus diff

Generated at unix=1778686114; window=last 24h; job=beacon

**Aggregation:**
- Counters/`_total`/`_count`/`_sum` → `sum by (instance) (increase(metric[24h]))` (24h total)
- Gauges (everything else, excluding `_bucket`) → `avg by (instance) (avg_over_time(metric[24h]))` (24h time-average)
- `_bucket` series are skipped (histogram internals; the `_sum`/`_count` carry the signal)

**Host pairs compared** (host_type label):
- `solo` (hoodi): `beta-solo` ↔ `feat2-solo`
- `semi` (hoodi): `beta-semi` ↔ `feat2-semi`
- `sas` (hoodi): `beta-sas` ↔ `feat2-sas`
- `mainnet-super` (mainnet): `beta-mainnet-super` ↔ `feat2-mainnet-super`

**Columns:** `host` is the host_type pair label.

**Known caveats / read-with-care:**
- A few names are gauges that end in `_total` (e.g. `lodestar_db_size_bytes_total`). `increase()` over 24h on these reports the growth (or noise from gauge resets), not a counter increment.
- Histogram `_bucket` series were skipped on purpose; `_sum` / `_count` carry the signal.
- `solo` / `semi` Hoodi nodes have very low base activity (few validators, often zero validator-monitor counters), so any non-zero spike there shows as a huge %.
- Some metrics only exist on one side at all (newly-added or removed). Those show empty cells on the missing side.
